rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    actions {
        While(Not(Is Game In Progress));
            Wait(0.03, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Pause Match Time;
        If(Compare(Current Map, ==, Map(Workshop Island Night)));
            Create HUD Text(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Custom String("{0}{1} ", Value In Array(Append To Array(String Split(Custom String(" Match Starting in # Le match commence dans # Spielstart in # Partida empezando en # La partida comienza en "), Global.lIllIlllIlll), String Split(Custom String(" Матч начнется через # Partida começa em "), Global.lIllIlllIlll)), (Local Player).IllIIllIllII), Global.IlIIIIIlIlll), Global.lllIIllllIIl, Global.lllIIllllIIl, Top, 4, Color(White), Null, Null, Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
            Start Rule(IIIIlIIIllIl, Restart Rule);
        Else;
            Wait(10, Ignore Condition);
            Set Match Time(99999);
            Destroy All HUD Text;
            Destroy All Progress Bar HUD Text;
            Create HUD Text(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Value In Array(Array(Custom String(" {0}, Current Map Unsupported! Please change the map to \"Workshop Island (Night)\"! ", Host Player), Custom String(" {0}, Carte actuelle non prise en charge ! Veuillez changer la carte en \"Île de la Forge Nuit\" ! ", Host Player), Custom String(" {0}, Aktuelle Karte nicht unterstützt! Bitte ändere die karte auf \"Workshop-Insel Nacht\"! ", Host Player), Custom String(" {0}, Mapa actual no es compatible! Cambie el mapa a \"Isla del Taller nocturno\"! ", Host Player), Custom String(" {0}, ¡Mapa actual no es compatible! ¡Cambie el mapa a \"Isla de Workshop noche\"! ", Host Player), Custom String(" {0}, Текущая карта не поддерживается! Пожалуйста, измените карту на \"Мастерская: остров ночь\"! ", Host Player), Custom String(" {0}, Mapa atual não suportado! Por favor, mude o mapa para \"Ilha do Workshop Noite\"! ", Host Player)), (Local Player).IllIIllIllII), Null, Null, Top, True, Color(White), Null, Null, Visible To and String, Default Visibility);
            Set Slow Motion(10);
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        IIIIlIIIllIl;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(llIIllllIIll, Last Text ID);
        Set Match Time(180);
        While(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll);
            Wait(Multiply(True, Global.llllIIllIlII), Ignore Condition);
            Modify Global Variable(IlIIIIIlIlll, Subtract, If-Then-Else(Is True For Any(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, And(And(Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 12), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))), (Current Array Element).IlIIIIIIllIl)), True, False));
        End;
        Destroy HUD Text(Global.llIIllllIIll);
        Destroy Effect(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI);
        Destroy Effect(Global.IlllIIIIlIIl);
        Destroy Effect(Global.IIllIlllIIIl);
        Destroy Effect(Global.lIIlllIllIlI);
        Destroy Icon(Global.IIllIIllIllI);
        Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
        Set Global Variable(IlIIIIIlIlll, Empty Array);
        Set Global Variable(lIllIlIIIIlI, Empty Array);
        Set Global Variable(IlllIIIIlIIl, Empty Array);
        Set Global Variable(IIllIlllIIIl, Empty Array);
        Set Global Variable(lIIlllIllIlI, Empty Array);
        Set Global Variable(IIllIIllIllI, Empty Array);
        Resurrect(Global.IlIlllIIllIl);
        Set Global Variable(llIIllllIIll, Empty Array);
        Set Global Variable(llIllIIlllll, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1), 2, False));
        Start Rule(lIIlllIlllIl, Restart Rule);
        Unpause Match Time;
        If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 3));
            Pause Match Time;
            While(And(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, Compare(Match Time, >, 10)));
                Set Match Time(Subtract(Match Time, True));
                Wait(0.75, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            While(Global.IIlllllIIIlI);
                Set Match Time(Subtract(Match Time, 0.1));
                Wait(0.075, Ignore Condition);
            End;
        End;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        IIllIIIIlIlI;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(IllllIIIIIII, False);
        While(Compare(Global.IllllIIIIIII, <=, 11));
            If(And(Compare(Count Of(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, And(Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 12), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))))), <, 3), Compare(Count Of(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, And(Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 12), Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element)))), <, Subtract(3, Count Of(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, And(Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 12), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element)))))))));
                Create Dummy Bot(Hero(Torbjörn), All Teams, Global.IllllIIIIIII, Null, Null);
            Else If(Or(Compare(Count Of(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, And(Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 12), Not(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element))))), >=, 3), Compare(Count Of(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, And(Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 12), Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element)))), >, 3)));
                Destroy Dummy Bot(All Teams, Global.IllllIIIIIII);
            End;
            Wait(0.05, Ignore Condition);
            Abort If(Compare(Global.IllllIIIIIII, ==, 11));
            Modify Global Variable(IllllIIIIIII, Add, 1);
            Wait(0.05, Ignore Condition);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(IIIlIIIlllIl, Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, (Current Array Element).lIllIllllIll));
        If(And(Global.IIIlIIIlllIl, Compare(Count Of(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 12))), >, 9)));
            Remove Player(First Of(Sorted Array(Global.IIIlIIIlllIl, Slot Of(Current Array Element))));
            Set Global Variable(IIIlIIIlllIl, Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, (Current Array Element).lIllIllllIll));
            Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
            Loop;
        End;
        Wait(2, Ignore Condition);
        Loop;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Player Left Match;
        All;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        Wait(0.5, Ignore Condition);
        Start Rule(IllIIlIllIII, Restart Rule);
        If(Compare(Total Time Elapsed, >, 30));
            Start Rule(llIlIIllIIll, Restart Rule);
    }
}

    }
}

    }

            End;
            Modify Player Variable(Global.lIllIlIIIIIl, IlIllllIlIlI, Add, 1);
            Wait(0.03, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Global.lIllIlIIIIIl, lllIIIIIIIlI, Custom String("{0}{1}{2}", (Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lIllIllllIIl, Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lIllIllllIIl, True), Custom String("{0}{1}{2}", Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lIllIllllIIl, 2), Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lIllIllllIIl, 3), Custom String("{0}{1}", Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lIllIllllIIl, 4), Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lIllIllllIIl, 5)))));

    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        lIIlllIlllIl;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(lIllllIIIllI, 100);
        If(And(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, !=, 1), Compare(Global.IllIIIIllIll, ==, 52)));
            Modify Global Variable(lIllIllllIIl, Append To Array, First Of(Global.lIllIllllIll));
            Modify Global Variable(lIllIllllIll, Remove From Array By Index, False);
            Modify Global Variable(IllIIIIllIll, Subtract, 1);
        End;
        If(And(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, !=, 1), Compare(Global.llllIIIIlIIl, ==, 12)));
            Modify Global Variable(IlIllllIlIlI, Append To Array, First Of(Global.lllIIIIlllll));
            Modify Global Variable(lllIIIIlllll, Remove From Array By Index, False);
            Modify Global Variable(llllIIIIlIIl, Subtract, 1);
        End;
        If(Global.IIIIllllIIIl);
            Set Global Variable(IIIIllllIIll, Global.IIIIllllIIIl);
            Set Global Variable(llIlIIllIIll, 0.2);
        Else If(Global.IIIlIIllIlll);
            Set Global Variable(IIIIllllIIll, Global.IIIlIIllIlll);
            Set Global Variable(llIlIIllIIll, 0.2);
        Else If(Compare(Global.llIllIIlllll, ==, 5));
            If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1));
                Set Global Variable(IIIIllllIIll, Random Value In Array(Array(106, 107, 114)));
            Else;
                Set Global Variable(IIIIllllIIll, Random Value In Array(Remove From Array(Global.IlIllllIlIlI, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 2), Array(113, 115), Empty Array))));
                Modify Global Variable(llllIIIIlIIl, Add, 1);
            End;
        Else;
            If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1));
                Set Global Variable(IIIIllllIIll, Random Value In Array(Array(1, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 10, 13, 14, 18, 19, 27, 31, 34, 37, 43, 45, 59)));
            Else;
                Set Global Variable(IIIIllllIIll, Random Value In Array(Remove From Array(Remove From Array(Global.lIllIllllIIl, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.lIIlIIlIIllI, !=, 2), Array(9, 10, 11, 12, 13, 14, 15, 23, 24, 25, 26, 27, 29, 30, 32, 33, 36, 38, 39, 40, 41, 42, 45, 46, 47, 48, 49, 51, 52, 53, 54, 55, 56, 57, 58, 60, 61, 62, 63, 64, 65), Array(1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, 16, 17, 18, 19, 20, 21, 22, 28, 31, 34, 35, 37, 43, 44, 50, 59))), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 2), Array(3, 4, 9, 10, 26, 32, 33, 36, 43, 53, 54, 57, 58, 64), Empty Array))));
                Modify Global Variable(IllIIIIllIll, Add, 1);
            End;
        End;
        Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
        Loop If(Not(Global.IIIIllllIIll));
        Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
        Set Global Variable(lIIlIIlIIlII, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIIIllllIIll, >=, 101), 30, If-Then-Else(Value In Array(Global.llIIIIIIllII, Global.IIIIllllIIll), Value In Array(Global.llIIIIIIllII, Global.IIIIllllIIll), 5)));
        Preload Hero(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), <, 12)), Value In Array(Global.IlllIllIIIIl, Global.IIIIllllIIll));
        Preload Hero(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Compare(Slot Of(Current Array Element), >=, 12)), Value In Array(Global.IlIIIIIllIll, Global.IIIIllllIIll));
        If(Compare(Global.IIIIllllIIll, >=, 101));
            Small Message(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Custom String("{0}{1}{0}", Icon String(Fire), Value In Array(Append To Array(String Split(Custom String(" Boss Time! [Worth 3 Score] # C'est l'heure du Boss ! [3 Points] # Boss Zeit! [Wert: 3 Punkte] # Hora del Jefe! [Vale 3 puntos] "), Global.lIllIlllIlll), String Split(Custom String(" ¡Hora del Jefe! [Vale 3 puntos] # Время босс-раунда! [Дает 3 очка] # Hora do boss! [Vale 3 pontos] "), Global.lIllIlllIlll)), (Local Player).IllIIllIllII)));
            If(And(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, !=, 1), Not(Global.IIIlIIllIlll)));
                Modify Global Variable(IlIllllIlIlI, Remove From Array By Value, Global.IIIIllllIIll);
                Modify Global Variable(lllIIIIlllll, Append To Array, Global.IIIIllllIIll);
            End;
            Set Global Variable(llIllIIlllll, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1), 2, False));
        Else;
            If(And(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, !=, 1), Not(Global.IIIIllllIIIl)));
                Modify Global Variable(lIllIllllIIl, Remove From Array By Value, Global.IIIIllllIIll);
                Modify Global Variable(lIllIllllIll, Append To Array, Global.IIIIllllIIll);
            End;
            Modify Global Variable(llIllIIlllll, Add, 1);
            If(Compare(Global.lIIlIIlIIllI, !=, 2));
                Modify Global Variable(lIIlIIlIIllI, Add, 1);
            Else;
                Set Global Variable(lIIlIIlIIllI, False);
            End;
        End;
        If(Global.IIIIllllIIIl);
            Set Global Variable(IllIIlIllIII, Global.IIIIllllIIIl);
        Else If(Global.IIIlIIllIlll);
            Set Global Variable(IllIIlIllIII, Global.IIIlIIllIlll);
        Else;
            Start Rule(lIlIIIIllIII, Restart Rule);
        End;
        Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
        Call Subroutine(llIllIIIlIlI);
        If(Compare(Count Of(Global.IlllIlIlIllI), ==, True));
            Call Subroutine(IllIllIlIIIl);
        End;
        If(Compare(Global.IIIIllllIIIl, ==, Global.IIIIllllIIll));
            Set Global Variable(IIIIllllIIIl, False);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IIIlIIllIlll, ==, Global.IIIIllllIIll));
            Set Global Variable(IIIlIIllIlll, False);
        End;
        Set Global Variable(IllIIlIllIII, Global.IIIIllllIIll);
        Set Global Variable(IlIllIlIIllI, True);
        Set Player Variable(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, IllIllIlIIIl, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIIIllllIIll, >=, 101), Global.lIIlIIlIIlII, 99));
        If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1));
            Modify Player Score(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, And(Not(Or((Current Array Element).lIllIllllIll, (Current Array Element).IlIIIIIIllIl)), Compare(Score Of(Current Array Element), <, Add(Global.lllllllIllll, 3)))), If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIIIllllIIll, >=, 101), 2, True));
        End;
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        Set Global Variable(llIllIllIlll, True);
        Chase Global Variable At Rate(lIllllIIIllI, False, Multiply(Divide(100, Global.lIIlIIlIIlII), Global.IlIIIIIlllll), None);
        While(Global.IllIIlIllIII);
            Wait(Multiply(True, Global.llllIIllIlII), Ignore Condition);
            Abort If(Not(Global.lIIlIIlIIlII));
            Modify Global Variable(lIIlIIlIIlII, Subtract, 1);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllIIllIllII, -1);
        Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
        If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), ==, 12));
            Set Global Variable(lIllIlIIIIIl, Event Player);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, IIlIlllIllII, True);
            If(Is Assembling Heroes);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, lllIIIIIIIlI, Global.IIIIIllllIlI);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIIllIlIIIlI, Global.IIIIIllllIlI);
            Else;
                Start Rule(IllIIlIllIII, Restart Rule);
            End;
            Start Rule(IlIllIlIIllI, Restart Rule);
            Start Rule(IlIllllIlIlI, Restart Rule);
        End;
        While(Not(Is Game In Progress));
            Wait(0.03, Ignore Condition);
        End;
        If(Not(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player)));
            Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Event Player, Hero(Torbjörn));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, IIlIIllllIIl, Custom String("{0}", Event Player));
        End;
        If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), <, 12));
            Set Max Health(Event Player, 10);
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Disable Built-In Game Mode Respawning(Event Player);
        Start Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player, Custom String("​"));
        If(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllIIllIllII, False);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlIIIIIIllIl, True);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIlIllIIIllI, True);
        End;
        If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), >=, 12));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIIlllIlllIl, True);
            If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), ==, 13));
                Set Global Variable(IlllIlIllIlI, Event Player);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIIllIlIllII, True);
            End;
        Else If(Not(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player)));
            Enable Death Spectate All Players(Event Player);
            Enable Death Spectate Target HUD(Event Player);
            Set Primary Fire Enabled(Event Player, False);
            Set Secondary Fire Enabled(Event Player, False);
            Set Melee Enabled(Event Player, False);
            Set Ability 1 Enabled(Event Player, False);
            Set Ability 2 Enabled(Event Player, False);
            Set Ultimate Ability Enabled(Event Player, False);
            Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
            If(Compare(Custom String("{0}", Event Player), ==, Custom String("​")));
                Set Gravity(Event Player, False);
                Set Invisible(Event Player, All);
                Teleport(Event Player, Vector(0, 800, 0));
                Start Rule(IllllllIIIIl, Restart Rule);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllIIllIllII, False);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIllIllllIll, True);
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                Clear Status(Event Player, Phased Out);
                Set Status(Event Player, Null, Knocked Down, 9999);
                Set Status(Event Player, Null, Unkillable, 9999);
                Set Player Score(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1), 99, -1));
                Abort;
            End;
            Stop Forcing Dummy Bot Name(Event Player);
            If(And(Global.IIlIlIllIIIl, Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1)));
                Set Player Score(Event Player, 99);
            End;
            Start Facing(Event Player, Direction From Angles(Value In Array(Array(15, 30, 45, 60, 75, 90, 105), Add(True, Index Of Array Value(String Split(Custom String("Champ de tir#Trainingsbereich#Práctica de combate#Campo de pruebas#УЧЕБНЫЙ ПОЛИГОН#Campo de Treinamento"), Global.lIllIlllIlll), Custom String("{0}", Map(Practice Range))))), False), 9999, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
            Wait(0.1, Ignore Condition);
            While(Compare((Event Player).IllIIllIllII, ==, -1));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllIIllIllII, Index Of Array Value(Array(1500, 3000, 4500, 6000, 7500, 9000, 10500), Round To Integer(Multiply(Horizontal Facing Angle Of(Event Player), 100), To Nearest)));
                Wait(0.05, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Start Facing(Event Player, Forward, 9999, To World, None);
            Start Rule(IllIIlIllIII, Restart Rule);
            While(Not(Or(Or(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire)), Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire))), Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact)))));
                Wait(0.03, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Stop Facing(Event Player);
            If(Not(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact))));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlIIIIIIllIl, True);
            End;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIlIllIIIllI, True);
            While(Or(Global.IlIllIlIIllI, Not((Event Player).IlIIIIIIllIl)));
                Wait(0.05, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Create In-World Text(If-Then-Else(And(And(And(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, !=, 2), Global.IIlIlIllIIIl), Is Alive(Event Player)), Or(And(Not(Global.IlIllIlIIllI), Compare(Global.llIlIIllIIll, <=, 0.35)), Compare(Score Of(Event Player), ==, Global.lllllllIllll))), Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Empty Array), Custom String(" \n▼"), Add(Update Every Frame(Eye Position(Event Player)), Multiply(Up, Subtract(1.2, If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Local Player), <=, 16), Subtract(0.592, Update Every Frame(Multiply(Distance Between(Event Player, Local Player), 0.037))), False)))), 2.2, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To Position and Color, If-Then-Else(Compare(Score Of(Event Player), >=, 16), Global.lIllIlIlIlIl, If-Then-Else(Compare(Score Of(Event Player), >=, 13), Global.llIIlIIlllIl, If-Then-Else(Compare(Score Of(Event Player), >=, 10), Global.IIIIIlIlllIl, If-Then-Else(Compare(Score Of(Event Player), >=, 7), Global.lIIIIllIlIll, If-Then-Else(Compare(Score Of(Event Player), >=, 4), Global.lIlIlIlIllIl, Global.lIIllIIIIlll))))), Default Visibility);
            Create In-World Text(If-Then-Else(And(And(And(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, !=, 2), Global.IIlIlIllIIIl), Is Alive(Event Player)), Or(And(Not(Global.IlIllIlIIllI), Compare(Global.llIlIIllIIll, <=, 0.35)), Compare(Score Of(Event Player), ==, Global.lllllllIllll))), Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Empty Array), Custom String("{0}\n ", Score Of(Event Player)), Add(Update Every Frame(Eye Position(Event Player)), Multiply(Up, Subtract(1, If-Then-Else(Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Local Player), <=, 16), Subtract(0.4, Update Every Frame(Multiply(Distance Between(Event Player, Local Player), 0.025))), False)))), 2.2, Clip Against Surfaces, Visible To Position and String, Color(White), Default Visibility);
            If(Global.IIlIlIllIIIl);
                If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1));
                    Set Player Score(Event Player, Add(Global.lllllllIllll, 3));

                    Set Player Score(Event Player, Round To Integer(Multiply(Global.lllllllIllll, 0.7), Down));
    }

    }

        Set Global Variable(lIlIllIlIlIl, False);
        Set Global Variable(IlIIlllIlllI, False);
        If(Compare(Global.IIlIIllIIlll, !=, 1));
            Set Global Variable(IIlIIllIIlll, True);
        Else;
            Start Rule(lIlIllIIIllI, Restart Rule);
    }

        Ongoing - Global;

        Global.IIlIIllIIlll == True;

    }
    actions {
        Start Rule(IIIlIlllIIlI, Restart Rule);
        Wait(Multiply(0.3, Global.llllIIllIlII), Abort When False);
        While(Or(Is Button Held(Host Player, If-Then-Else(Has Spawned(Host Player), Button(Primary Fire), Button(Ability 1))), Is Button Held(Global.lIlIIIlIIllI, Button(Primary Fire))));
            Start Rule(IIIlIlllIIlI, Restart Rule);
            Wait(Multiply(0.05, Global.llllIIllIlII), Ignore Condition);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Global;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.IlIllIlIIllI == True;
    }
    actions {
        Abort If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, >=, 101));
        If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 2));
            Set Move Speed(Global.llIlllIlllII, 200);
            Create Effect(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Sphere, Global.llIIlIIlllIl, False, 16, Visible To);
            Modify Global Variable(IlllIlIlIllI, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
        Else If(Array Contains(Array(3, 4), Global.IllIIlIllIII));
            Set Damage Dealt(Global.llIlllIlllII, Absolute Value(10000));
            Set Damage Received(Global.llIlllIlllII, 100);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 7));

    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).lIIlllIlllIl == True;
        Global.IlIllIlIIllI == True;
        Global.IllIIlIllIII < 101;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), >=, 12));
            If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 10));
                Set Damage Dealt(Event Player, 0.01);
                Teleport(Event Player, Global.IllllllIIIIl);

                If((Event Player).lIIllIlIllII);
                    Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
                Else If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), ==, 14));
                    Wait(0.4, Ignore Condition);
                End;
                While(Global.IllIIlIllIII);
                    If((Event Player).IIlIlllIllII);
                        Set Global Variable(IlIIIIIlIlll, Sorted Array(Global.llIlllIlllII, Score Of(Current Array Element)));
                        Set Global Variable(lIllIlIIIIlI, Index Of Array Value(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Last Of(Sorted Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Score Of(Current Array Element)))));
                        Wait(0.05, Abort When False);

                    Else If((Event Player).lIIllIlIllII);
                        Wait(0.05, Abort When False);
                        Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Value In Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Subtract(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI, True)));
                    Else;
                        Wait(0.05, Abort When False);
                        Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Value In Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Subtract(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI, 2)));
                    End;

                End;

                    Wait(0.05, Ignore Condition);
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Value In Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Subtract(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI, True)));
                Else;

                End;
                Start Forcing Throttle(Event Player, True, True, False, True, False, True);
                Create Effect(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Sphere, Global.llIIlIIlllIl, Event Player, 4, Visible To Position and Radius);

                Set Move Speed(Event Player, 130);
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);

                Start Rule(IlIIIlIIllll, Restart Rule);
                Teleport(Event Player, Random Value In Array(Global.lIIlIIIIlIIl));
                Start Rule(lIIlIIIIlIIl, Restart Rule);
                Wait(Multiply(4.9, Global.llllIIllIlII), Ignore Condition);
                Kill(Players Within Radius(Event Player, 4, All Teams, Off), Event Player);
                Play Effect(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Good Explosion, Global.lIIIIllIlIll, Event Player, 32);
            Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 16));
                Start Facing(Event Player, Direction Towards(Eye Position(Event Player), (Event Player).IllllllIIIIl), 200, To World, Direction and Turn Rate);
                Start Forcing Throttle(Event Player, 0.4, True, False, True, False, True);

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).lIIlllIlllIl == True;
        Global.IlIllIlIIllI == True;
        Global.IllIIlIllIII >= 101;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), >=, 12));
            If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 102));
                If((Event Player).IIlIlllIllII);
                    Set Global Variable(IIllIlllIIIl, 40);
                    Set Global Variable(lIIlllIllIlI, 2);
                End;
                Start Rule(IlIIIlIIllll, Restart Rule);
                Wait(True, Ignore Condition);
                Start Rule(lIIlIIIIlIIl, Restart Rule);
                Create Effect(If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, !=, 100), Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Empty Array), Light Shaft, Global.llIIlIIlllIl, Subtract(Event Player, Up), Global.lIIlllIllIlI, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Modify Global Variable(IlllIlIlIllI, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
                If((Event Player).IIlIlllIllII);
                    Chase Global Variable At Rate(lIIlllIllIlI, False, Multiply(0.1, Global.IlIIIIIlllll), None);
                End;
                While(Global.IllIIlIllIII);
                    Set Ability Cooldown(Event Player, Button(Ability 1), False);

            Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 115));

                Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, False);
                Wait(Add(0.4, Multiply(0.05, Slot Of(Event Player))), Ignore Condition);
                Create Icon(If-Then-Else(And(Is Alive(Event Player), (Event Player).IllllllIIIIl), Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Empty Array), Event Player, Asterisk, Visible To and Position, Color(Sky Blue), False);
                Modify Global Variable(IlllIlIlIllI, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);
                Create Effect(Remove From Array(If-Then-Else(And(Is Alive(Event Player), (Event Player).IllllllIIIIl), Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Empty Array), Event Player), Bad Aura, Color(Sky Blue), Event Player, 0.5, Visible To Position and Radius);
                Modify Global Variable(IlllIlIlIllI, Append To Array, Last Created Entity);

rule ("") {
    event {
        Player Dealt Damage;
        All;
        All;
    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Victim, IlIIIlIIllll, Event Player);
        If(Array Contains(Array(4, 10), Global.IllIIlIllIII));
            Kill(Event Player, Null);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 28));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
            Set Primary Fire Enabled(Event Player, False);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 32));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
            Wait(0.03, Ignore Condition);
            Set Status(Victim, Null, Phased Out, Multiply(1.95, Global.llllIIllIlII));
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 36));
            Modify Player Variable At Index(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Slot Of(Victim), Add, 1);
            If(Is True For Any((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, Compare(Current Array Element, >=, 20)));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, Players In Slot(Index Of Array Value((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, Last Of(Sorted Array((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, Current Array Element))), All Teams));
                Set Status((Event Player).llIllIIIlIlI, Null, Frozen, True);
                Set Status((Event Player).llIllIIIlIlI, Null, Phased Out, True);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Modify Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Remove From Array By Value, Last Of(Sorted Array((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, Current Array Element)));
            End;
        Else If(And(And(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 41), Compare(Victim, !=, Event Player)), Compare(Event Ability, ==, Button(Ability 2))));
            Kill(Victim, Event Player);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 42));
            If(Compare(Slot Of(Victim), >=, 12));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Set Primary Fire Enabled(Event Player, False);
            Else;
                Kill(Event Player, Null);
            End;
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 55));
            Kill(Victim, Event Player);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 56));
            Apply Impulse(Victim, Direction Towards(Event Player, Add(Position Of(Victim), Vector(0, 0.3, 0))), 30, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 60));
            If(Compare(Hero Of(Victim), ==, Global.IlIIIIIlIlll));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Set Primary Fire Enabled(Event Player, False);
            Else;
                Kill(Event Player, Null);
            End;
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 62));
            If(Compare(Global.IIllIlllIIIl, ==, 12));
                Kill(Victim, Event Player);
            Else;
                Kill(Event Player, Null);
            End;
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 64));
            Apply Impulse(Victim, Direction Towards(Event Player, Add(Position Of(Victim), Vector(0, 0.3, 0))), 30, To World, Cancel Contrary Motion);
        Else If(Array Contains(Array(104, 110), Global.IllIIlIllIII));
            If(Event Was Critical Hit);
                Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Add((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, 40), Multiply(200, Global.IlIIIIIlllll), None);
            Else;
                Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Add((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, 20), Multiply(100, Global.IlIIIIIlllll), None);
            End;
            Wait(0.25, Ignore Condition);
            If(Compare((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, >, 100));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, 100);
            End;
            Chase Player Variable At Rate(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, False, Multiply(12, Global.IlIIIIIlllll), None);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 107));
            Set Global Variable(IlIIIIIlIlll, Victim);
        Else If(And(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 108), Compare(Event Ability, ==, Button(Ability 1))));
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIIlIIIIlIIl, Ray Cast Hit Position(Victim, Add(Victim, Vector(0, -5, 0)), Null, Global.IlIlllIIllIl, False));
        Else If(And(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 113), Compare(Victim, !=, Event Player)));
            Modify Player Variable(Victim, IllllllIIIIl, Subtract, Multiply(3, Global.IlIIIIIlllll));
            If(And(And(Compare((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, <, 100), (Event Player).IllllllIIIIl), Not(Is In Alternate Form(Event Player))));
                Modify Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Add, 1);
    }

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        (Event Player).lIllIllllIll == False;
        Global.llIlIlllIIll == True;
    }
    actions {
        Abort If(Not((Event Player).IlIIIIIIllIl));
        If(Not(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player)));
            If(And((Event Player).lIIlllIlllIl, Or(Is Alive(Event Player), (Event Player).IlllIIlIIIIl)));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllIIllIIlII, True);
                If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1));
                    Start Rule(llIIIIIIIIIl, Restart Rule);
                End;
            Else If((Event Player).lIIlllIlllIl);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIIlIIIlIIlI, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).IllIllIlIIIl, <=, 9), 3, If-Then-Else(Compare((Event Player).IllIllIlIIIl, <=, 19), 2, True)));
                If(Compare((Event Player).lIIlIIIlIIlI, >=, 2));
                    Modify Player Score(Event Player, Subtract((Event Player).lIIlIIIlIIlI, True));
                End;
            End;
            If(And(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1), Compare(Score Of(Event Player), >, Add(Global.lllllllIllll, 3))));
                Set Player Score(Event Player, Add(Global.lllllllIllll, 3));
            Else If(Compare(Score Of(Event Player), <, Round To Integer(Multiply(Global.lllllllIllll, 0.7), Down)));
                Set Player Score(Event Player, Round To Integer(Multiply(Global.lllllllIllll, 0.7), Down));
            End;
        End;
        Wait(Multiply(0.05, Slot Of(Event Player)), Ignore Condition);
        If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), <, 12));
            Set Max Health(Event Player, 10);
        End;
        Start Forcing Player To Be Hero(Event Player, Hero(Torbjörn));
        Start Rule(IIlIlllIllII, Restart Rule);
        Abort If(Is Dummy Bot(Event Player));
        If(Or(Compare(Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), >=, 10), Compare(Y Component Of(Position Of(Event Player)), <, -0.01)));
            Start Rule(lIIllIlIllII, Restart Rule);
    }
}

    }
    actions {
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, Index Of Array Value(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, First Of(Sorted Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element)))));
        If(Or(Compare((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, ==, Global.IIllIlllIIIl), If-Then-Else(Global.IIllIIllIllI, False, Compare((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, ==, Global.lIIlllIllIlI))));
            Teleport(Event Player, Vector(0, 1000, 0));
            Set Gravity(Event Player, False);
            Start Rule(IllllllIIIIl, Restart Rule);
            If(Compare((Event Player).IllllllIIIIl, ==, Global.lIIlllIllIlI));
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, 2);
            Else;
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, 1);
            End;
        Else;
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, 0);
            Teleport(Event Player, Vector(0, -1000, 0));
        End;
        Abort If(Global.IIllIIllIllI);
        Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("{0}{1}{2}", Value In Array(String Split(Custom String("You get #Vous gagnez #Du erhälst #Ganas #Consigues #Вы получили #Você ganha "), Global.lIllIlllIlll), (Local Player).IllIIllIllII), (Event Player).llIllIIIlIlI, Value In Array(String Split(Custom String(" score!# point(s)# Punkte!# puntos!# puntos!# очков!# pontos!"), Global.lIllIlllIlll), (Local Player).IllIIllIllII)));
        If(Compare((Event Player).llIllIIIlIlI, ==, 2));
            While(Global.IllIIlIllIII);
                Wait(0.2, Ignore Condition);
            End;
            Modify Player Score(Event Player, True);
        End;
        Wait(0.1, Abort When False);
        Loop If Condition Is True;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        Torbjörn;
    }
    conditions {
        Array Contains(Array(19, 20), Global.IllIIlIllIII) == True;
        Global.llIllIllIlll == True;
        Or(Or(Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Primary Fire)), Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Secondary Fire))), Is Button Held(Event Player, Button(Interact))) == True;
        Is Alive(Event Player) == True;
        (Event Player).IlllIIlIIIIl == False;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Distance Between(Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Multiply(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 3)), Vector(-0.5, 1.3, False)), <=, 0.3));
            If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 19));
                If(Not(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Else;
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                End;
            Else;
                If(Not(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Else;
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                End;
            End;
        Else If(Compare(Distance Between(Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Multiply(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 3)), Vector(0.5, 1.3, False)), <=, 0.3));
            If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 19));
                If(Compare(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, ==, 1));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Else;
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                End;
            Else;
                If(Compare(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI, ==, 1));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Else;
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                End;
            End;
        Else If(Compare(Distance Between(Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Multiply(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 3)), Vector(-0.5, 0.8, False)), <=, 0.3));
            If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 19));
                If(Compare(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, ==, 2));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Else;
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                End;
            Else;
                If(Compare(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI, ==, 2));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Else;
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                End;
            End;
        Else If(Compare(Distance Between(Add(Eye Position(Event Player), Multiply(Facing Direction Of(Event Player), 3)), Vector(0.5, 0.8, False)), <=, 0.3));
            If(Compare(Global.IllIIlIllIII, ==, 19));
                If(Compare(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, ==, 3));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Else;
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
                End;
            Else;
                If(Compare(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI, ==, 3));
                    Set Player Variable(Event Player, IlllIIlIIIIl, True);
                Else;
                    Kill(Event Player, Null);
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        Wrecking Ball;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.IllIIlIllIII == 114;
        Global.llIllIllIlll == True;
    }
    actions {
        Set Knockback Received(Event Player, 80);
        While(Global.IllIIlIllIII);
            If((Event Player).IIlIlllIllII);
                Set Global Variable(IlIIIIIlIlll, Sorted Array(Global.llIlllIlllII, Score Of(Current Array Element)));
                Set Global Variable(lIllIlIIIIlI, Index Of Array Value(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Last Of(Sorted Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Score Of(Current Array Element)))));
                Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, Last Of(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll));
            Else If((Event Player).lIIllIlIllII);
                Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, Value In Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Subtract(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI, True)));
            Else;
                Wait(0.016, Ignore Condition);
                Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, Value In Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Subtract(Global.lIllIlIIIIlI, 2)));
            End;
            Teleport(Event Player, Global.IllllllIIIIl);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, 100);
            Wait(Multiply(4, Global.llllIIllIlII), Ignore Condition);
            Kill(Filtered Array(Global.llIlllIlllII, Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element), <=, Subtract(7, Multiply(Count Of(Global.llIlllIlllII), 0.3)))), Event Player);
            Play Effect(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Good Explosion, Global.lIIIIllIlIll, Event Player, Multiply(2.5, Subtract(7, Multiply(Count Of(Global.llIlllIlllII), 0.3))));
        End;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        Mei;
    }
    conditions {
        Global.IllIIlIllIII == 115;
        Or(Or(Or(Is True For All(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Compare(Distance Between(Event Player, Current Array Element), >=, 1.5)), Not(Is Crouching(Event Player))), Compare((Event Player).llIllIIIlIlI, ==, 100)), Is Dead(Event Player)) == True;
    }
    actions {
        Stop Chasing Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI);
        Set Move Speed(Event Player, If-Then-Else(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 4), 150, 100));
        Set Jump Enabled(Event Player, True);

            Set Player Variable(Event Player, IllllllIIIIl, True);
            Set Player Variable(Event Player, lIlIIIIllIII, Index Of Array Value(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, First Of(Sorted Array(Global.IlIIIIIlIlll, Distance Between(Position Of(Event Player), Current Array Element)))));

            Play Effect(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Good Pickup Effect, Color(Sky Blue), Position Of(Event Player), True);
            Destroy Effect(Value In Array(Global.IlllIIIIlIIl, (Event Player).lIlIIIIllIII));
            Modify Global Variable(IlllIIIIlIIl, Remove From Array By Index, (Event Player).lIlIIIIllIII);
            Modify Global Variable(IlIIIIIlIlll, Remove From Array By Index, (Event Player).lIlIIIIllIII);
        End;
        Set Player Variable(Event Player, llIllIIIlIlI, False);
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        IIIlIIllIlII;
    }
    actions {
        Set Global Variable(llIIIllllIIl, False);
        Start Rule(IlIIlllIllIl, Restart Rule);
        Call Subroutine(llIllIIIlIlI);
        Wait(0.4, Ignore Condition);
        Set Global Variable(llIIIllllIIl, True);
        Set Global Variable(IlIlIllIlIlI, True);
        Modify Global Variable(lIllIIlIlIIl, Add, 1);
        If(Compare(Global.lIllIIlIlIIl, ==, 2));
            Modify Global Variable(lIIlIllIlIll, Append To Array, First Of(Global.llllIlIIIlll));
            Modify Global Variable(llllIlIIIlll, Remove From Array By Index, False);
            Set Global Variable(lIllIIlIlIIl, True);
        End;
        Modify Global Variable(lIIlIllIlIll, Remove From Array By Value, Global.IIlllllIIIlI);
        Modify Global Variable(llllIlIIIlll, Append To Array, Global.IIlllllIIIlI);
        If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 1));
            Set Match Time(90);
            Set Player Score(Filtered Array(Global.IlIlllIIllIl, Or(Is Dummy Bot(Current Array Element), (Current Array Element).lIllIllllIll)), 99);
        Else If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 3));
            Set Slow Motion(75);
            Set Global Variable(llllIIllIlII, 0.75);
            Set Global Variable(IlIIIIIlllll, 1.334);
        End;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Subroutine;
        IlIIlllIllIl;
    }
    actions {
        If(Global.lIIIlIllllll);
            Set Global Variable(IIlllllIIIlI, Global.lIIIlIllllll);
            Set Global Variable(lIIIlIllllll, False);
        Else;
            While(Not(Global.llIIIllllIIl));
                Set Global Variable(IIlllllIIIlI, Random Value In Array(Global.lIIlIllIlIll));
                Wait(Global.llIlIIllIIll, Ignore Condition);
                Abort If(Global.llIIIllllIIl);
            End;
        End;
    }
}

rule ("") {
    event {
        Ongoing - Each Player;
        All;
        All;
    }
    conditions {
        Has Spawned(Event Player) == True;
        Global.IIlllllIIIlI == True;
        Global.llIIIllllIIl == True;
    }
    actions {
        If(Compare(Slot Of(Event Player), <, 12));
            Small Message(Event Player, Custom String("{0}{1}{2}{0}", Icon String(Fire), Value In Array(String Split(Custom String(" Special Mode: # Mode spécial : # Spezial-Modus: # Modo especial: # Modo especial: # Особый режим: # Modo especial: "), Global.lIllIlllIlll), (Local Player).IllIIllIllII), Value In Array(Array(Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lIIlllIllIlI, Global.IIlllllIIIlI), Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).IIllIIllIllI, Global.IIlllllIIIlI), Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).IlllIlIlIllI, Global.IIlllllIIIlI), Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lIlllllIIIII, Global.IIlllllIIIlI), Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).lllIIllIIlIl, Global.IIlllllIIIlI), Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).IlIIIIlIllIl, Global.IIlllllIIIlI), Value In Array((Global.lIllIlIIIIIl).llIlIlllIIll, Global.IIlllllIIIlI)), (Local Player).IllIIllIllII)));
            If(And((Event Player).IlIIIIIIllIl, Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 2)));
                Set Invisible(Event Player, All);
            Else If(And(And((Event Player).IlIIIIIIllIl, Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 4)), Not(Is Using Ability 2(Event Player))));
                Set Move Speed(Event Player, 150);
            End;
        End;
        If(Compare(Global.IIlllllIIIlI, ==, 3));
            Start Modifying Hero Voice Lines(Event Player, 0.85, False);
    }
}
